<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">огры́зть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogrýztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одергивать.html>одёргиваемый</a> (18381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***одалживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживать</a> (29802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolžítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odálživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lend <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to allow to be used temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">мари́на <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомый.html>незнако́мым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́дям</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Marína nikogdá ne <b>odálživajet</b> dénʹgi neznakómym ljúdjam.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Marina never <b>lends</b> money to strangers.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to borrow <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to receive (something) temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иногда.html>иногда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдохнуть.html>отдохну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́де</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On inogdá <b>odálžival</b> u druzéj údočku, kogdá xotél otdoxnútʹ na priróde.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He sometimes <b>borrowed</b> a fishing rod from friends when he wanted to relax outdoors.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The difference between "to lend" and "to borrow" is determined by the context and the usage of prepositions and cases, e.g. "he lends me money" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>" is a dative case) and "he borrows money from me" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживает</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a>" is used with the genitive case).</li>
<li>The object of lending/borrowing is normally in the accusative but can also be in the genitive case, especially in the negative clauses.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">both senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одолжа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odolžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:занимать.html>занима́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zanimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to lend</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаймы.html>взаймы́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">davátʹ vzajmý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ссужа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ssužátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>to loan</i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to borrow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взаймы.html>взаймы́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bratʹ vzajmý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживающий</a> (29802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odálživajuščij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривающий</a> (25294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***одарить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a> (13916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дарить.html>дари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">darítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одаря́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одаривать.html>ода́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give presents
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ть</a></b> кого́-либо че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odarítʹ</b> kovó-libo čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to present someone with something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endow <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одарить.html>одари́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразный.html>разнообра́зными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бностями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">priróda <b>odaríla</b> jevó raznoobráznymi sposóbnostjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nature has endowed him with a variety of talents</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a> (12491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одевать.html>одева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></b>)

***одевшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеться.html>оде́вшийся</a> (4693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***одежда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a> (1011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from Old Church Slavonic, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*odeďa</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежа.html>одёжа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odjóža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odéžda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clothes, clothing, garments</li>
<li>surfacing, top dressing</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odjóžka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжек</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clothes

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежка.html>одёжке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречать.html>встреча́ют</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уму́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провожать.html>провожа́ют</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po odjóžke vstrečájut, a po umú provožájut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">clothes count for first impressions only</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a> (11438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oderžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win, to gain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžátʹ</b> verx nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prevail over someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžátʹ</b> pobédu nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a victory over someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Припадок <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">одержал</span> юношу полные трое суток с переменчивою силою; на третье утро, начиная чувствовать в себе более крепости, он вставал с постели, когда ему сказали, что в прихожей дожидается старая служанка вдовы. </span></li>

***одерживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a> (29676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odérživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win, to gain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odérživatʹ</b> verx nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prevail over someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одерживать.html>оде́рживать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odérživatʹ</b> pobédu nad kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win a victory over someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a> (12027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oderžímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>possessed <i>(by)</i>, obsessed (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одержать.html>одержи́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oderžímyj</b> stráxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ridden by fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
